<tbody valign=”top”> <tr><th>what:</th><td><p dir=”auto”>Field lists map field names to field bodies, like database records. They are often part of an extension syntax. They are an unambiguous variant of RFC 2822 fields.</p> </td> </tr> <tr><th>how arg1 arg2:</th><td><p dir=”auto”>The field marker is a colon, the field name, and a colon.</p> <p dir=”auto”>The field body may contain one or more body elements, indented relative to the field marker.</p> </td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <a name=”user-content-option-lists”></a> <h3 dir=”auto”><a id=”user-content-option-lists” class=”anchor” aria-hidden=”true” href=”#option-lists”><svg class=”octicon octicon-link” viewBox=”0 0 16 16” version=”1.1” width=”16” height=”16” aria-hidden=”true”><path fill-rule=”evenodd” d=”M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z”></path></svg></a><a href=”#id37”>Option Lists</a></h3> <p dir=”auto”>For listing command-line options:</p> <table frame=”void” rules=”none”>

<tbody valign=”top”> <tr><td> <kbd><span>-a</span></kbd></td> <td>command-line option “a”</td></tr> <tr><td> <kbd><span>-b <var>file</var></span></kbd></td> <td>options can have arguments and long descriptions</td></tr> <tr><td> <kbd><span>–long</span></kbd></td> <td>options can be long also</td></tr> <tr><td> <kbd><span>–input=<var>file</var></span></kbd></td> <td>long options can also have arguments</td></tr> <tr><td colspan=”2”> <kbd><span>–very-long-option</span></kbd></td> </tr> <tr><td> </td><td><p dir=”auto”>The description can also start on the next line.</p> <p dir=”auto”>The description may contain multiple body elements, regardless of where it starts.</p> </td></tr> <tr><td> <kbd><span>-x</span>, <span>-y</span>, <span>-z</span></kbd></td> <td>Multiple options are an “option group”.</td></tr> <tr><td> <kbd><span>-v</span>, <span>–verbose</span></kbd></td> <td>Commonly-seen: short &amp; long options.</td></tr> <tr><td colspan=”2”> <kbd><span>-1 <var>file</var></span>, <span>–one=<var>file</var></span>, <span>–two <var>file</var></span></kbd></td> </tr> <tr><td> </td><td>Multiple options with arguments.</td></tr> <tr><td> <kbd><span>/V</span></kbd></td> <td>DOS/VMS-style options too</td></tr> </tbody> </table> <p dir=”auto”>There must be at least two spaces between the option and the description.</p> <a name=”user-content-literal-blocks”></a> <h3 dir=”auto”><a id=”user-content-literal-blocks” class=”anchor” aria-hidden=”true” href=”#literal-blocks”><svg class=”octicon octicon-link” viewBox=”0 0 16 16” version=”1.1” width=”16” height=”16” aria-hidden=”true”><path fill-rule=”evenodd” d=”M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z”></path></svg></a><a href=”#id38”>Literal Blocks</a></h3> <p dir=”auto”>Literal blocks are indicated with a double-colon (“::”) at the end of the preceding paragraph (over there <code>–&gt;</code>). They can be indented:</p> <pre>if literal_block:

text = ‘is left as-is’ spaces_and_linebreaks = ‘are preserved’ markup_processing = None

</pre> <p dir=”auto”>Or they can be quoted without indentation:</p> <pre>&gt;&gt; Great idea! &gt; &gt; Why didn’t I think of that? </pre> <a name=”user-content-line-blocks”></a> <h3 dir=”auto”><a id=”user-content-line-blocks” class=”anchor” aria-hidden=”true” href=”#line-blocks”><svg class=”octicon octicon-link” viewBox=”0 0 16 16” version=”1.1” width=”16” height=”16” aria-hidden=”true”><path fill-rule=”evenodd” d=”M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z”></path></svg></a><a href=”#id39”>Line Blocks</a></h3> <div dir=”auto”> <div dir=”auto”>This is a line block. It ends with a blank line.</div> <div dir=”auto”> <div dir=”auto”>Each new line begins with a vertical bar (“|”).</div> <div dir=”auto”>Line breaks and initial indents are preserved.</div> </div> <div dir=”auto”>Continuation lines are wrapped portions of long lines; they begin with a space in place of the vertical bar.</div> <div dir=”auto”> <div dir=”auto”>The left edge of a continuation line need not be aligned with the left edge of the text above it.</div> </div> </div> <div dir=”auto”> <div dir=”auto”>This is a second line block.</div> <div dir=”auto”><br></div> <div dir=”auto”>Blank lines are permitted internally, but they must begin with a “|”.</div> </div> <p dir=”auto”>Take it away, Eric the Orchestra Leader!</p> <blockquote> <div dir=”auto”> <div dir=”auto”>A one, two, a one two three four</div> <div dir=”auto”><br></div> <div dir=”auto”>Half a bee, philosophically,</div> <div dir=”auto”> <div dir=”auto”>must, <em>ipso facto</em>, half not be.</div> </div> <div dir=”auto”>But half the bee has got to be,</div> <div dir=”auto”> <div dir=”auto”><em>vis a vis</em> its entity. D’you see?</div> <div dir=”auto”><br></div> </div> <div dir=”auto”>But can a bee be said to be</div> <div dir=”auto”> <div dir=”auto”>or not to be an entire bee,</div> <div dir=”auto”> <div dir=”auto”>when half the bee is not a bee,</div> <div dir=”auto”> <div dir=”auto”>due to some ancient injury?</div> <div dir=”auto”><br></div> </div> </div> </div> <div dir=”auto”>Singing…</div> </div> </blockquote> <a name=”user-content-block-quotes”></a> <h3 dir=”auto”><a id=”user-content-block-quotes” class=”anchor” aria-hidden=”true” href=”#block-quotes”><svg class=”octicon octicon-link” viewBox=”0 0 16 16” version=”1.1” width=”16” height=”16” aria-hidden=”true”><path fill-rule=”evenodd” d=”M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z”></path></svg></a><a href=”#id40”>Block Quotes</a></h3> <p dir=”auto”>Block quotes consist of indented body elements:</p> <blockquote> <p dir=”auto”>My theory by A. Elk. Brackets Miss, brackets. This theory goes as follows and begins now. All brontosauruses are thin at one end, much much thicker in the middle and then thin again at the far end. That is my theory, it is mine, and belongs to me and I own it, and what it is too.</p> <p dir=”auto”>—Anne Elk (Miss)</p> </blockquote> <a name=”user-content-doctest-blocks”></a> <h3 dir=”auto”><a id=”user-content-doctest-blocks” class=”anchor” aria-hidden=”true” href=”#doctest-blocks”><svg class=”octicon octicon-link” viewBox=”0 0 16 16” version=”1.1” width=”16” height=”16” aria-hidden=”true”><path fill-rule=”evenodd” d=”M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z”></path></svg></a><a href=”#id41”>Doctest Blocks</a></h3> <div class=”highlight highlight-text-python-console notranslate position-relative overflow-auto” dir=”auto” data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=”&gt;&gt;&gt; print ‘Python-specific usage examples; begun with &quot;&gt;&gt;&gt;&quot;’ Python-specific usage examples; begun with &quot;&gt;&gt;&gt;&quot; &gt;&gt;&gt; print ‘(cut and pasted from interactive Python sessions)’ (cut and pasted from interactive Python sessions)”><pre>&gt;&gt;&gt; For others, please see <a href=”http://docutils.sourceforge.net/docs/ref/rst/directives.html” rel=”nofollow”>http://docutils.sourceforge.net/docs/ref/rst/directives.html</a>.</p> <a name=”user-content-topics-sidebars-and-rubrics”></a> <h4 dir=”auto”><a id=”user-content-topics-sidebars-and-rubrics” class=”anchor” aria-hidden=”true” href=”#topics-sidebars-and-rubrics”><svg class=”octicon octicon-link” viewBox=”0 0 16 16” version=”1.1” width=”16” height=”16” aria-hidden=”true”><path fill-rule=”evenodd” d=”M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z”></path></svg></a><a href=”#id49”>Topics, Sidebars, and Rubrics</a></h4> <div dir=”auto”> <p dir=”auto”>Sidebar Title</p> <p dir=”auto”>Optional Subtitle</p> <p dir=”auto”>This is a sidebar. It is for text outside the flow of the main text.</p> <p dir=”auto”>This is a rubric inside a sidebar</p> <p dir=”auto”>Sidebars often appears beside the main text with a border and background color.</p> </div> <div dir=”auto”> <p dir=”auto”>Topic Title</p> <p dir=”auto”>This is a topic.</p> </div> <p dir=”auto”>This is a rubric</p> <a name=”user-content-compound-paragraph”></a> <h4 dir=”auto”><a id=”user-content-compound-paragraph” class=”anchor” aria-hidden=”true” href=”#compound-paragraph”><svg class=”octicon octicon-link” viewBox=”0 0 16 16” version=”1.1” width=”16” height=”16” aria-hidden=”true”><path fill-rule=”evenodd” d=”M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z”></path></svg></a><a href=”#id50”>Compound Paragraph</a></h4> <div dir=”auto”> <p dir=”auto”>This paragraph contains a literal block:</p> <pre>Connecting… OK Transmitting data… OK Disconnecting… OK </pre> <p dir=”auto”>and thus consists of a simple paragraph, a literal block, and another simple paragraph. Nonetheless it is semantically <em>one</em> paragraph.</p> </div> <p dir=”auto”>This construct is called a <em>compound paragraph</em> and can be produced with the “compound” directive.</p> <a name=”user-content-id13”></a> <h3 dir=”auto”><a id=”user-content-comments-1” class=”anchor” aria-hidden=”true” href=”#comments-1”><svg class=”octicon octicon-link” viewBox=”0 0 16 16” version=”1.1” width=”16” height=”16” aria-hidden=”true”><path fill-rule=”evenodd” d=”M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95
